name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted December 17, 2023
msg:Accommodation is not cheap compared to surrounding Emeishan, but it is really worth it. Absolutely a great place for families with children.
The entire hotel covers a large area and is manor-type, giving it the feel of a Southeast Asian resort. The park is very large, and there is a shuttle bus on call, but you can also take a walk for exercise, and the quiet scenery is good. The hotel also has Yanjiyou Bookstore, where children can play and adults can read very well.
The hotel has a large scenic lake. The white swans and black swans are both fat and friendly. There is also a cute little white horse for children to experience. Two ponies, Little Snowball and Little Rainbow, Little Snowball is docile, and Little Rainbow is naughty.
The accommodation is equipped with a butler who is very considerate and can help with anything. The rooms are large, and the garden-view double rooms are equipped with bathtubs and viewing balconies. On the first day, I used my rights to upgrade to the Lake-view Si Mawu Villa. On the second floor, there is a special viewing platform, which is very quiet. The hotel also gave children special toothbrushes, toothpaste, and small bathrobes.
There are not many hot spring pools, but the temperature is very good and the water is clean. The middle pool has cold water in winter and is unusable. It should be better in summer.
The breakfast is very rich, with many Chinese and Western varieties of egg cakes, tofu cakes and so on. The style of the restaurant is good, and it is divided into Chinese restaurant and Western restaurant. The Chinese restaurant has various types of food. I was too lazy to go out to eat, so I ate fried rice in a Chinese restaurant. The bacon fried rice and egg fried rice were both great. The buffet on Saturday night is also rich, including small hot pot, stilted beef, seafood, steak, lamb chops, barbecue sausages, and many desserts. It should be said that the chef's skills are good and the taste is quite good.
The hotel order also included a travel photography package with three free photos. The photographer did a great job! The children have always been afraid to get close to the swans, and it‚Äôs a pity that I didn‚Äôt take a photo with the swans.
The hotel is indeed a family-focused hotel. It organizes various parent-child activities every day to keep the children from getting bored. It also gave out gold coins for the children to check in and win gold coins during their stay. The children were very active and finally exchanged the gold coins for a panda tree-climbing pen, which was very interesting. A sense of accomplishment. There are also paid go-kart rides and climbs, so children can have a lot of fun without leaving the hotel.
It was my first time to book this hotel with the attitude of giving it a try, and it far exceeded my expectations. The kids all said this hotel was great! I booked a high-speed rail round trip and there is a dedicated shuttle bus, which is very convenient. Overall, I am very satisfied and will come back in the summer!
Facilities: hot springs, swimming pools, Chinese restaurants, Western restaurants, parent-child activities, playgrounds, bookstores, wine bars, go-karts, horseback riding, gyms, outdoor climbing, travel photography
Hygiene: clean
Environment: The park is large, beautiful and quiet
Service: Very considerate
Enjoy 30 minutes of free vacation photography: three free photos, great shots!
"Playing in the Snow and Bathing in the Hot Spring Season" all-weather parent-child activities: There are many activities, with various types of activities suitable for children.
Outdoor open-air hot spring pool: The temperature is just right, suitable for washing away the fatigue of the day before going to bed.
